 40-year-old Pullela Gopichand, India's head national coach and 18-year-old Pusarla Venkat Sindhu, one of his most promising disciples, sit side-by-side on a bench in the gym on the ground floor of his Badminton Academy in Hyderabad
 sindhu mahila badminton main duniya kii sheersh 15 khiladinnon main shumaar hai
 The two are talking about how the game took a shape, how it evolved
 senior editor amarnath ke
 In a meeting with Menon, he discussed Prakash Padukone's victory in the 1980 All England Championship
 yah bhi charchaa kaa vishay bana ki 2001 main padukon kaa kartab dohraane ke baavjood apni tej yuva shishyaa sina nehwal ke ubharne tak gopichand kaise vah asar chhodie main naakaam rahe
 And why Indus is a rising star? pulela gopichandprakash padukon sar ke jamaane se hi bharat kaa badminton kaa khel kamobesh ek hi khilaadi ke boote chalata aayaa he
 He won several titles including the 1980 All England Championship
 uske baad ek dashak to aisa laga ki is khel main ab koi khaas aakarshan nahin rah gaya he
 But in the 1990s, the interest of people once again arose
 uske baad mujhe ek mauka mila or 2001 main achaanak maine bhi ol england championships jeet lee
 But i could not stay on top for long
 prakaash sar ke banaae duusare recordon ko toduya to dur, main unki barabari bhi na kar sakaa
 i could not get too many opportunities due to injury and some other reasons
 uske baad ek kharaab daur gujara
 But in 2008, Saina Nehwal raised hopes again
 par bhartiya badminton ke liye yah utana acha nahin rahaa jitna ki sina ke liye
 Last year we saw Sindhu becoming the Asian Junior Champion and this year saw her win the Malaysian Grand Prix and also win a medal at the World Championships
 iske baad log bhartiya badminton par gambhirtha se dhyaan dene ko majaboor ho gaye
 This is a new beginning because now this game of ours is no longer limited to a single person
 yahi vajah he ki is saal pehle indian badminton lig ke ran-ap main darshak is khel ke badalte mizaaj par tippanee karte sune gaye
 That badminton is now seen in a mature state
 pusarala venkat sindhugopi sar, aisa lagata he ki aapke daur main khelon main kariyar bananaa bilkul alag rahaa hoga
 Explain what were the main challenges at that time? Gopichand was getting a lot of encouragement and sponsorship of cricket and a little bit of hockey till the 1982 Asian Games in the early 1980s
 cricket ke alaava duusare khelon ke protsaahan or infrastracchar banane par lagane vaala kul prayaas or dhan cricket ke kshetra main lagane vaale prayaas or dhan kaa bahut maamuli hissaa hua karata tha
 But any comparison with cricket is meaningless
 pichley do dashakon main yah sab kuch badal gaya he
 Our facilities and training skills can be compared to some of the best facilities and training skills in the world in this sport
 par haa, olympic swarna padak ke liye ab bhi utani bhukh nahin he, jitani bharat jaise vishaal desh main honi chahie
 In this case, perhaps we have to learn from China
 sindhuaj kii taarikh main badminton main china kii chunauti bahut majboot he
 If you are playing against any of their players, then it becomes a completely different game
 aapke samay main vishwa str ke pratispardhiyon kaa saamana karnaa nishchit taur par or bhi mushkil rahaa hoga
 See Gopichand, if you want to do something good in badminton, then you will have to beat the Chinese
 china kii ek mahaan diwaar badminton ke kshetra main bhi he
 Saina has won just one game out of every three of the 60 games played against the Chinese
 purushon main pi
 Kashyap has won only one game out of every five played against him
 purush or mahila badminton main duniya ke sheersh 25 khiladinnon main paanch bhartiya hai jabaki china ke saat khilaadi hai or ve sabhi sheersh 10 khiladinnon main shumaar hai
 They are truly tremendous
 philhal sindhu kaa record shandaar he kyonki unhone chiniyon ke khilaaf khele gaye apane aadhe match jite hai
 Sindhuun's commitment is really worth watching
 unki ranneeti or mushkil kshanon main apane khel ko oonchai par le jane kaa unka tarika unhen dusron ke mukaable behatar khilaadi bana detaa he
 Sometimes they try to give some points in the beginning so that we are happy and lose our concentration
 gopichandmagar sindhu unke is jaal main bahut zyada nahin fansi hai
 This has happened because we are also studying the way our opponents play, recording it and making the necessary corrections to deal with each player
 sindhuyaheen par yoga or dhyaan bahut madad karte hai
 i remember my parents at 4 in the morning
 30 baje jagaa diya karte the or kareeb 30 kilometre travel kar mujhe academy chhodie aayaa karte the
 It was very difficult for me because i had to leave school and then i did not like mental training
 mujhe lagata tha ki sirf badminton khelnaa hi paryaapt he
 After that Gopi sir took command and completely changed me and many other players
 gopichandaisa isliye kyonki 2001 main ol england championships jeetne ke baad maine tay kiya ki vaigyanik drushtikon se suvidhaon or prashikshan kii vyavastha kar badminton ke liye kaaphi kuch or kiye jane kii jarurat he
 In 2003, the Andhra Pradesh government gave me five acres of rocky land on a 45-year lease to start the academy
 lekin use viksit karne ke liye paise nahin the
 i had to mortgage my family property to get a loan
 yonnex or ek rishtedaar kii madad se 2008 tak hamane ise har tarah kii suvidhaon se las ek academy ke rup main viksit kar liya
 Both my parents have been national basketball players and they have been telling people how during their youth there was a complete lack of training facilities for any sport
 or ve mujhe bataate hai ki sikanderabad se aakar academy se 2 kilometre kii duuri par bas jane se main yahaan kii suvidhaon kaa adhiktam istemaal karne main kaamyaab ho pai
 Gopichand: i think full dedication is the first need
 yahi vajah he ki main har kisi se time-teble or prashikshan niyamon kaa kadai se paalan karwaata hum
 Such basic tendencies create determination
 isamen do raay nahin ki koi bhi do khilaadi ek jaise nahin hote
 Every player is unique in himself with a different mindset, different dealings, physical height and a personal style of play
 ek vyapak prashikshan kaarykram mahatvapurn hota he jisamen aap gati, chapaltaa or fitness vagairah viksit karte hai
 To gain strength in Sindhukhel, i had to give up chocolate, take green powder of Spirulina, sea-weed and some other foods
 is jaise kai or tyaag kathin prashikshan kaa hissaa hai
 It also involves putting a little bit on the temptation to watch movies
 gopichandahamane khiladinnon kii ek samrudh-sampann nursery se acchhee fasal kaatani shuru bhi kar di he
 Like Sindhu, there is a young plant of Indian sportspersons who are doing well and it is just a couple of years late to give good results
 vyaktigat spardhaa ke khiladinnon ke alaava mujhe yakeen he ki hamaari dubles vaali kuch jodissan jald hi jabardast chhap chhodia shuru kar dengi
 The Indusindian Badminton League (IBL) has been a great experience and this has brought the sport into focus
 gopi sar, kya aapako lagata he ki is tarah kaa prayog lambey daur main upyogi hone ja rahaa he?gopichandyah ek jabardast mauka he
 IBL can contribute to making badminton more popular than it is today
 lekin baat sirf itani hi nahin he
 More and more of our players get to experience competition by playing with and against the best players in the world
 sarvshereshth khiladinnon ko badminton khelte hue dekhnaa ek sukhad anubhav he

 yah bhavishya ke liye seekhney kii jameen ke taur par kaam karata he

 ) rajendra raav peshey se ejeeniyar rahe kintu man kissagoi main ramata rahaa

 aakhri dinon main un par likhaa unke sansmaran bahut bedhak hai

 avadh kii maati kii khushboo kaa anand lete hue us par gahan shabdakachitr likh diya

 ab tak unke darjanon kahani sangrah prakashit hue jinamein asaty ke prayog, nausikhia, shesh yatra, doodh ke daant, suuli upar sej piya kii, koyala bhai naa raakh, paap punya se pare, kitne shirin hai tere lab ki pramukh hai

 ab vah rang nirdeshkon ke hawaale he

 ve kehete hai, ''lakh suvidha janak ho laptop magar kalam-dawaat se moh abhi baaki he

 '' ek samay tha ki koyala bhai naa raakh kii kathasiris kii log raah dekha karte the
 Kola Bhai Na Rakh: The Story Series Kokela Bhai Na Rash narrates the story of Rajendra Rao: "the life of writers is not free from irony
 kaishorya se lekar yuvavastha tak meraa man aas-paas ke aise logon ko dekh kar pighalta rahaa jinhone apane jivan ko sajaane-sanvaarane main koi kasar nahin chodi
 Be ready to dig the mountain, but nothing was found except for the night's bed
 khwab kaanch ke khilonon kii tarah tuutate-bikharate rahe or ummid bhi nahin bachi
 When i started writing, they were molded into narrative characters and after writing their grief stories, let's finally share their grief
 "yah katha shrinkhalaa 'koyala bhai na raakh' ke naam se saptahik hindustan main dharawahik chhapi or pathakon kaa dhyaan khinchne main safal rahi
 Of publishers too
 yah to tha auron ke dukhon ko anubhuti ke str par mahasoos karke rachanaatmakataa kii disha grahan karnaa
 But, when later, much later, a mountain of sorrow broke over me, i came to know exactly how all those, charcoal and ash characters would have spent their lives suffering unbearable pain
 ''is kitaab ke prakashit hone kaa bhi dilachasp kissa he
 Rao says, "I was a new writer in those days
 meri ek kahani ko pard kar saptahik hindustan ke sampadak manohar shyaam joshi ji ne kaha ki hamen aisi das kahaniyaan dijiye jinhen ham dharawahik rup se chhaapenge
 The stories of 'coal bhai na ash' liked Vishwanath ji of Rajpal publication so much that he sent him a proposal to publish it in book form
 raajapaal un dinon bade prakaashak the
 This in itself was a big encouragement for a new writer
 kitaab chhapi or bahut acchhee railty bhi mili
 This is the year of 1975
 tab ke sampadak or prakaashak kis tarah yuva lekhakon ko protsaahit or prerit karte the
 "after being unpublished for a long time, now this book has been published again with Rajpal & Sons
 kuch logon ke liye kahani likhnaa ek ghante yaa do ghante kaa khel hota he
 It would not be difficult to guess by seeing the frequent storytellers
 par may 2019 main nayaa gyanoday main ai kahani 'baith jaao' ko likhane main unhen kaaphi samay laga
 He says, "in the last four decades, there has never been so much difficulty in writing a story as was experienced in putting this Darun saga of savitri-satyavan on paper
 iske liye pathar kaa kalejaa hona chahie
 "recently, his famous story 'chokher Bali' was staged at Kamani Auditorium in Delhi which was directed by Tikam Joshi
 rajendra raav ke shaukarajendra raav ke shauk niraale hai
 They remember the figs and sharifs of their house very much, they say the noor of Sharafat, in our garden
 jaise sharife kii sharafat is lekhak ke charitra kaa bhi ek hissaa ho

 pehle patni thim to har vakt kii bolchaal kii saathi

 kabhi-kabhi is akelepan kaa maarmik izhaar bhi ve karte hai

 ve gaalib ko pasand karte hai

 bahut acchhee lagi to lage haath us par ek tippaani likh kar fasebuk par taank di

 muradanagar kii smritiyon ko karine se taanka

 oonche-oonche maal to pani bharte se lage uske saamne

 ''rajendra raav sukh dukh ke har lamhe ko ek bhokta or drashtaa donon bhav se darj karte hai
 All human juices are present within them
 har lamhaa kahani kii sambhaavna liye hai, jaise ashok vaajapeyi ke liye shahar ab bhi ek sambhaavna he
 But as said, he may be interested in reading, reading and writing all the genres, but he is a storyteller
 isliye kahani kii duniya main aaj bhi unki apni pahchaan he

 rajendra raav kii kahaniyandekhane main sahaj, sanjeeda kintu- baton se sahitya main gahare page lekhak kaa ahsaas dilaane vaale rajendra raav ne kanpur jaise shramikon ke mahanagar ke ek kone main baith kar sahitya ke maanchitr par apni jagah darj karai he
 His stories, reports have been a time boom
 kalam monjane ke liye kolkata tak kii galiyon ke chakkar lagane ke unke paas bahuterey anubhav hai tathaa ejineering kii shushk duniya se sambhddha rahete hue bhi maanviyata ke swapn kii sulagati dhimi lau kii roshni main unhone anek paatro charitron or sthitiyon ko sirja he tathaa yah siddh kiya he ki jis tarah jindagi har jagah maujuud he, kahaniyaan bhi vaise hi har jagah bikhri hui hai, bas unhen sahejane or pakadaney kii jarurat he
 If you want to go through any one of his stories, then you can understand Rajendra Rao's authoritative mood
 kahani or kavita main kathy kaa bhi apana fishan or apana daur hota he

 prem kavitaaon or kahaniyon kaa vasant har vaktar sarsabj hota he

 apni har kahani se chaunkaa dene vaale
 The inner atmosphere on the world machine is extremely human
 abhi kuch hi baras pehle hi ek lambii khamoshi ke baad rajendra raav kahaniyon kii duniya main laute to phir ekaek un dinon kii yaad dilaa di jab assi ke dashak ke daur kii chuninda patrikaon ke chand charchit kahanikaron main ve hua karte the
 After the publication of Shift Kahani in Kahani Patrika in 71, he did not look back and grew from one story to another
 nausikhia, shift, koyala bhai na raakh, asaty ke prayog, doodh ke daant or prem kahaniyon kii siries suuli upar sej piya kii aadi
 Meanwhile, two of his novels also appeared but his pace in the stories continued
 gaye chaar paanch saal main unhone apni duusari pari main pandrah se zyada kahaniyaan likhi hai
 As i have already written, Rajendra Rao's world has also been a world of mechanical engineering, where he worked between machines, earning a living and gaining world knowledge
 unka man beshak un mashiinon ke bich na lagata rahaa ho par anek kahaniyaan unhone us masini jindagi ke bich se uthaain tathaa kahani main aise viral maahaul kii sristi kii jahaan koi saadhaaran kahanikar nahin pahunch saktaa tha
 Rajendra Rao also wrote all the stories of Prem
 agle janam main, maut ke baad, sudhaa or suresh, mud kar nahin dekha, pyaar kii parachhaaiyaan, pyaar denge dil kaa dard lenge, paap punya se pare aisi hi kahaniyaan hai
 There is also the perplexity of love, the deceitful love of Cashory, the long letters written in love, the sighs and tears
 asal baat yah ki unke paatr adarshavaad kii choukhat par dam nahin todate balki varjanaaon kii simaaon kaa atikaraman karte najar aate hai
 But while he has done subtle scanning of the hearts of lovers in his stories, he has also taken many valuable moments of life from the middle of the machine routine

 In today's era, all the poets are coming from the world of storytellers, science technicians and management, who are breaking the new ground of expression
 rajendra raav ne bataur ejeeniyar kaarkaane main kaam kiya, choubees ghante shift incharge rahe to masini kolahal or utpaadan ke laabh haani ke ganit main ulajhate hue unke samvedansheel man kaa chatapataana swahabhavik hi he
 Most of the stories of this story of Rajendra Rao are also a product of his experiences
 par ve kehete hai, masini duniya main hone kaa arth yah nahi ki vahaan antarvaiyaktik sambandhon ke rang chatkh nahin hai yaa us duniya main prem nahin he, samvednaa nahin he, jivan nahin he
 Rather we can see this fact with full splendor in stories like shift, novice, rest of history, infiltration and gourd oil etc
 kissagoi sabake bas kii nahin hoti
 Along with the narration of the incident, the characters' emotions are also kept in a precise manner that in which the storyteller's own vision can be seen in the language of idioms, it happens less

 For example, the father is a philanthropic in succession
 ve bete ke jariye niyamit taur par ek apahiz ko kuch khaane kaa saamaan bhijwate hai jo shahar main ho rahe sadak nirmaan ke saath darbadar hoti rahati he or jarurat se zyada leti nahin
 When the son gave the reference to his father, he took things
 par ant main pita ji kii mrityu ke baad use kuch dene ke liye aata he or tab jo samvaad unke bich hota he vah ankhen sajal kar detaa he
 As if the son had inherited the spirit of philanthropy
 isamen padonniti par kaha gaya vaakya dhyatavya he: "kisi bhi naukari pesha ke jivan main yah atmontkarsh kaa chirpratikshit pal hota he
 "how comfortable it is for a worker in gourd oil to speak in his pillow Kalam Jo Hai So Wali Ada: Babu, you urban men do not know how beneficial gourd oil is

 vaidiki hinsa main daaru or murge ke cholii daaman ke rishtein kii charchaa karte hue kahani kaa nayak kahata he, ekaadh baar maansaahaari hone kii koshish kii magar jab khalabalaakar antadiyaan baahar aane lageen to tobaa kar lee maine maansaahaar se or doston ne hitopadesh se

 ek ajeeb si laalasaa jaag uthati he, jisaki tulana sirf vishuddh vaasana se kii ja sakati he
 The whole legal violence story of Puri is full of such tight idiocy
 thenga, landure, labhed, nautankibaj, khalas, suptan paurush aisi shabdaawalee ki pard kar kahanikar kii pratibha kii daad deni padati he

 ' baaki itihaas main jisamen diarector ke visit or jiem ke karpshan kii charchaa he, usamen visit kii taiyaariyon main chaar chand lagane vaale katha nayak kaa uwach dekhie- "raturaat mere man se vifal prem se upji hataasha or nirviyata kii kalonch puchh gayi or ant:patal steel kii thali kii tarah jagamaga uthaa
 "the protagonist of the story in Shift says," i also wanted to open the body like a plant
 "rajendra raav kii kahaniyaan saadhaaran kahaniyaan nahin, jivan samay or samaaj se judy kahaniyon hai
 These are stories of mills, factories, of relationships, of love, of struggle, of philanthropy, of rituals, of Indian travels, of mechanical life, of nightly colors, and of human beings coming down on dogs in their swamisthi
 
 har kahani kisi na kisi makasad se likhi gayi he
 Every sentence of his derives from a prolonged penance of experience
 kahani ke cathopakathan or andajebyan kii jitani tarif kii jaay kam he
 Rajendra Rao is not a satirist but somewhere in his narration, shiny and agile sentences like Shrilal Shukla shine
 jaise kabhi shrilaal ji ne visrampur kaa sant main kaha he: sarkari murde bahut kharch karaate hai
 In Rajendra Rao's stories too, such sentences can be seen from a distance
 vaidiki hinsa main kahanikar kahata he, "behudepan kii intiha sharaab ho, saath main chikan ho udaane ko, bas ho gaya grand celibrasion, is khatkarm main sabase pehle suuli chadhataa he saundaryabodh
 "needless to say that Rajendra Rao has tried his best to maintain this aesthetic sense in his anecdote so that neither boredom nor aesthetic decay
 kisi bhi ghatana yaa prasang ke chapper chappe par nigaah daalane vaale raav kii kahaniyaan isiilie padhane waalon ko vimugdh kar detii hai
 Prathamushpraya in stories: His stories are written in the first person, in which the narrator himself speaks
 vah kahin aagyaakaari putr ke rup main kartavya nirvaah se prerit he (uttaradhikaar) to kahin train main vatting tikat par jhooth bol kar avaidh yatra or asaty kaa prayog karte hue ek yatri ke rup main (asaty ke prayog), kahin shift main dauty par tainaat to kahin kaarkaane main ek nausikhia
 Somewhere as a person who wants to celebrate the smallest success of life (legal violence), somewhere as a young man in a lower middle-class life (gourd oil), somewhere he is liberated from his corporate job
 Ravi like (amar Nahi Yeh Pyaar) trying to pursue a coaching business with his father, as Sathish of Chhinomasta struggles for a job
 par stri paatr bhi maanviya gunon se bhare hai chaahe uttaradhikaar kii apaahijaa ho, lowki kaa tel kii maa hon, chinmasta kii maa hon, yaa amar nahin yah pyaar kii medha
 Their characters are memorable, non-enduring characters, even in unpleasant situations
 buraaiyon se ghire samaaj main bhi inke bheetar ek swapn he jise rajendra raav ne har kahani main ek dhimi lau ke rup main jinda rakhaa he
 This is the specialty of Rajendra Rao's stories that he is sure to experience the mechanical world but does not ignore the human aspect within it, always keeps it at the center of the stories
